\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em The S\+DL keyboard scancode representation. \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\subsection{Detailed Description}
Defines keyboard scancodes. 

\subsection{Enumeration Type Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777b}\label{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777b}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode}{SDL\_Scancode}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777b}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode}}}



The S\+DL keyboard scancode representation. 

Values of this type are used to represent keyboard keys, among other places in the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_s_d_l___keysym_ad47e9120a511e2efc7ec0c6d8a5ec51e}{key.\+keysym.\+scancode }} field of the \mbox{\hyperlink{union_s_d_l___event}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Event}} structure.

The values in this enumeration are based on the U\+SB usage page standard\+: \href{http://www.usb.org/developers/hidpage/Hut1_12v2.pdf}{\tt http\+://www.\+usb.\+org/developers/hidpage/\+Hut1\+\_\+12v2.\+pdf} \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+S\+L\+A\+SH@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+S\+L\+A\+SH}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}}\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+S\+L\+A\+SH@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+S\+L\+A\+SH}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777ba0ada7413e8a549d8a91d095789a3c138}\label{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777ba0ada7413e8a549d8a91d095789a3c138}} 
S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+S\+L\+A\+SH&Located at the lower left of the return key on I\+SO keyboards and at the right end of the Q\+W\+E\+R\+TY row on A\+N\+SI keyboards. Produces R\+E\+V\+E\+R\+SE S\+O\+L\+I\+D\+US (backslash) and V\+E\+R\+T\+I\+C\+AL L\+I\+NE in a US layout, R\+E\+V\+E\+R\+SE S\+O\+L\+I\+D\+US and V\+E\+R\+T\+I\+C\+AL L\+I\+NE in a UK Mac layout, N\+U\+M\+B\+ER S\+I\+GN and T\+I\+L\+DE in a UK Windows layout, D\+O\+L\+L\+AR S\+I\+GN and P\+O\+U\+ND S\+I\+GN in a Swiss German layout, N\+U\+M\+B\+ER S\+I\+GN and A\+P\+O\+S\+T\+R\+O\+P\+HE in a German layout, G\+R\+A\+VE A\+C\+C\+E\+NT and P\+O\+U\+ND S\+I\+GN in a French Mac layout, and A\+S\+T\+E\+R\+I\+SK and M\+I\+C\+RO S\+I\+GN in a French Windows layout. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+U\+S\+H\+A\+SH@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+U\+S\+H\+A\+SH}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}}\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+U\+S\+H\+A\+SH@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+U\+S\+H\+A\+SH}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777bac3a553bf8b10cc5fb62734c866e799e5}\label{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777bac3a553bf8b10cc5fb62734c866e799e5}} 
S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+U\+S\+H\+A\+SH&I\+SO U\+SB keyboards actually use this code instead of 49 for the same key, but all O\+Ses I\textquotesingle{}ve seen treat the two codes identically. So, as an implementor, unless your keyboard generates both of those codes and your OS treats them differently, you should generate S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+S\+L\+A\+SH instead of this code. As a user, you should not rely on this code because S\+DL will never generate it with most (all?) keyboards. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+M\+I\+C\+O\+L\+ON@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+M\+I\+C\+O\+L\+ON}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}}\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+M\+I\+C\+O\+L\+ON@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+M\+I\+C\+O\+L\+ON}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777ba8784cfcaf0597143c194575787042952}\label{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777ba8784cfcaf0597143c194575787042952}} 
S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+M\+I\+C\+O\+L\+ON&\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+A\+P\+O\+S\+T\+R\+O\+P\+HE@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+A\+P\+O\+S\+T\+R\+O\+P\+HE}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}}\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+A\+P\+O\+S\+T\+R\+O\+P\+HE@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+A\+P\+O\+S\+T\+R\+O\+P\+HE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777ba3aeee9fe769cce606a77b30e6db468aa}\label{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777ba3aeee9fe769cce606a77b30e6db468aa}} 
S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+A\+P\+O\+S\+T\+R\+O\+P\+HE&\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+VE@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+VE}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}}\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+VE@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+VE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777ba98a95c705af01d280d8ce14146bdddae}\label{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777ba98a95c705af01d280d8ce14146bdddae}} 
S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+VE&Located in the top left corner (on both A\+N\+SI and I\+SO keyboards). Produces G\+R\+A\+VE A\+C\+C\+E\+NT and T\+I\+L\+DE in a US Windows layout and in US and UK Mac layouts on A\+N\+SI keyboards, G\+R\+A\+VE A\+C\+C\+E\+NT and N\+OT S\+I\+GN in a UK Windows layout, S\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON S\+I\+GN and P\+L\+U\+S-\/\+M\+I\+N\+US S\+I\+GN in US and UK Mac layouts on I\+SO keyboards, S\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON S\+I\+GN and D\+E\+G\+R\+EE S\+I\+GN in a Swiss German layout (Mac\+: only on I\+SO keyboards), C\+I\+R\+C\+U\+M\+F\+L\+EX A\+C\+C\+E\+NT and D\+E\+G\+R\+EE S\+I\+GN in a German layout (Mac\+: only on I\+SO keyboards), S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+S\+C\+R\+I\+PT T\+WO and T\+I\+L\+DE in a French Windows layout, C\+O\+M\+M\+E\+R\+C\+I\+AL AT and N\+U\+M\+B\+ER S\+I\+GN in a French Mac layout on I\+SO keyboards, and L\+E\+S\+S-\/\+T\+H\+AN S\+I\+GN and G\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+R-\/\+T\+H\+AN S\+I\+GN in a Swiss German, German, or French Mac layout on A\+N\+SI keyboards. \\

S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+U\+S\+B\+A\+C\+K\+S\+L\+A\+SH&This is the additional key that I\+SO keyboards have over A\+N\+SI ones, located between left shift and Y. Produces G\+R\+A\+VE A\+C\+C\+E\+NT and T\+I\+L\+DE in a US or UK Mac layout, R\+E\+V\+E\+R\+SE S\+O\+L\+I\+D\+US (backslash) and V\+E\+R\+T\+I\+C\+AL L\+I\+NE in a US or UK Windows layout, and L\+E\+S\+S-\/\+T\+H\+AN S\+I\+GN and G\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+R-\/\+T\+H\+AN S\+I\+GN in a Swiss German, German, or French layout. \\
